# Lessons Learned

## Session Lessons
- Supabase paused projects block schema dumps and linking operations.
- For this environment, Supabase direct DB hosts resolved to IPv6 and failed; pooler endpoints worked.
- For type generation, use Supabase CLI with project ref: `supabase gen types typescript --project-id <ref> --schema public > src/types/supabase.ts`.
- Avoid `supabase gen types --db-url ...` in this environment; it attempted a Docker-backed path and failed when Docker daemon was unavailable.
- Raw `pg_dump` output is not fully idempotent on Supabase; `CREATE SCHEMA` and `ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES` can fail.
- Applying dumps to Supabase requires filtering unsupported privilege statements.
- DB-first migrations can break app runtime immediately when code still references removed tables/columns.
- Cloudflare global API key must use `X-Auth-Key` + `X-Auth-Email`, not Bearer token.
- R2 bucket creation via API is straightforward, but S3 key management differs from API token handling.
- Always validate new R2 credentials with a real S3 request before using them in production envs.
- Keep `tasks/` ignored by default but force-add specific planning files when needed.
- When user is editing concurrently, avoid touching their changed files and commit only explicit pathspecs.
- When running Vitest with configs under `tests/`, execute from the `tests/` working directory (or adjust paths) so `setup.ts` resolves correctly.
- Vitest v4 constructor mocks must provide constructable implementations for class-like dependencies (for example, `new Resend(...)`).
- During gateway/OTP deprecations, remove stale route/service tests first, then re-baseline middleware and payment-flow assertions to current endpoints.
- Keep `tests/.env` synchronized with root env profile keys (including key-name mappings like publishable key aliases) before trusting test-suite results.

## Implementation Guardrails
- Keep schema and generated types in lockstep.
- Prefer `--project-id` generation from Supabase CLI as the default regeneration method for `src/types/supabase.ts`.
- Make payment callbacks idempotent before enabling live traffic.
- Use preview-first rollout with explicit drift checks between preview and production.
- Maintain a single migration runbook with exact commands and expected outputs.
- Keep deploy workflow env blocks aligned with active providers; stale secret keys in CI can silently rot release readiness.
- Prefer behavior-driven test expectations from current route/service contracts; update brittle response/message assertions immediately after contract changes.
- When Next.js route handlers accept `NextRequest`, integration/unit tests must call handlers with a request object; `GET()` without args can produce false 500 failures.
- For integrations touching third-party APIs (email/SMS), gate strict success assertions behind real credential detection and validate graceful fallback behavior for placeholder/local configs.

diff --git a/src/lib/utils/text.ts b/src/lib/utils/text.ts
new file mode 100644
index 0000000..1978b1f
--- /dev/null
+++ b/src/lib/utils/text.ts
@@ -0,0 +1,104 @@
+import {
+  parsePhoneNumberFromString,
+  type CountryCode,
+} from 'libphonenumber-js';
+
+const easternArabicDigitStart = 0x06f0;
+const arabicIndicDigitStart = 0x0660;
+
+export function normalizeDigits(text: string): string {
+  if (!text) return text;
+
+  return Array.from(text)
+    .map((char) => {
+      const code = char.charCodeAt(0);
+      if (
+        code >= easternArabicDigitStart &&
+        code <= easternArabicDigitStart + 9
+      ) {
+        return String(code - easternArabicDigitStart);
+      }
+      if (code >= arabicIndicDigitStart && code <= arabicIndicDigitStart + 9) {
+        return String(code - arabicIndicDigitStart);
+      }
+      return char;
+    })
+    .join('');
+}
+
+export function containsRightToLeftCharacters(text: string): boolean {
+  if (!text) return false;
+
+  return /[\u0590-\u08FF\uFB1D-\uFDFF\uFE70-\uFEFF]/.test(text);
+}
+
+export function isValidName(name: string): boolean {
+  const trimmed = name.trim();
+  if (!trimmed) return false;
+  if (trimmed.length > 120) return false;
+
+  return /^[\p{L}\p{M}][\p{L}\p{M}\s.'-]*$/u.test(trimmed);
+}
+
+export function normalizePhoneNumber(phone: string): string {
+  if (!phone) return phone;
+
+  const defaultCountry = (
+    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY || 'IR'
+  ).toUpperCase() as CountryCode;
+  let normalized = normalizeDigits(phone.trim()).replace(/[^\d+]/g, '');
+
+  normalized = normalized.replace(/(?!^)\+/g, '');
+  if (normalized.startsWith('00')) {
+    normalized = `+${normalized.slice(2)}`;
+  }
+
+  try {
+    const parsed = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry);
+    if (parsed?.isValid()) {
+      return parsed.number;
+    }
+  } catch {
+    return normalized;
+  }
+
+  return normalized;
+}
+
+export function getPhoneLookupCandidates(phone: string): string[] {
+  if (!phone) return [];
+
+  const defaultCountry = (
+    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY || 'IR'
+  ).toUpperCase() as CountryCode;
+  const normalized = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
+  const legacyNormalized = normalizeDigits(phone.trim()).replace(/[^\d+]/g, '');
+  const legacyWithoutPlus = legacyNormalized.replace(/\+(?=.)/g, '');
+  const nationalFormat = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry)
+    ?.formatNational()
+    .replace(/\D/g, '');
+
+  return Array.from(
+    new Set(
+      [normalized, nationalFormat, legacyNormalized, legacyWithoutPlus].filter(
+        (candidate): candidate is string => Boolean(candidate)
+      )
+    )
+  );
+}
+
+export function isValidPhoneNumber(phone: string): boolean {
+  if (!phone) return false;
+
+  const normalized = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
+  const defaultCountry = (
+    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY || 'IR'
+  ).toUpperCase() as CountryCode;
+
+  try {
+    const parsed = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry);
+    return parsed?.isValid() ?? false;
+  } catch {
+    return false;
+  }
+}

export function isValidName(name: string): boolean {
  const trimmed = name.trim();
  if (!trimmed) return false;
  if (trimmed.length > 120) return false;

  return /^[\p{L}\p{M}][\p{L}\p{M}\s.'-]*$/u.test(trimmed);
}

export function normalizePhoneNumber(phone: string): string {
  if (!phone) return phone;

  const defaultCountry = (
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY || 'US'
  ).toUpperCase() as CountryCode;
  let normalized = normalizeDigits(phone.trim()).replace(/[^\d+]/g, '');

  normalized = normalized.replace(/(?!^)\+/g, '');
  if (normalized.startsWith('00')) {
    normalized = `+${normalized.slice(2)}`;
  }

  try {
    const parsed = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry);
    if (parsed?.isValid()) {
      return parsed.number;
    }
  } catch {
    return normalized;
  }

  return normalized;
}

export function getPhoneLookupCandidates(phone: string): string[] {
  if (!phone) return [];

  const defaultCountry = (
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY || 'US'
  ).toUpperCase() as CountryCode;
  const normalized = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
  const legacyNormalized = normalizeDigits(phone.trim()).replace(/[^\d+]/g, '');
  const legacyWithoutPlus = legacyNormalized.replace(/\+(?=.)/g, '');
  const nationalFormat = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry)
    ?.formatNational()
    .replace(/\D/g, '');

  return Array.from(
    new Set(
      [normalized, nationalFormat, legacyNormalized, legacyWithoutPlus].filter(
        (candidate): candidate is string => Boolean(candidate)
      )
    )
  );
}

export function isValidPhoneNumber(phone: string): boolean {
  if (!phone) return false;

  const normalized = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
  const defaultCountry = (
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY || 'US'
  ).toUpperCase() as CountryCode;

  try {
    const parsed = parsePhoneNumberFromString(normalized, defaultCountry);
    return parsed?.isValid() ?? false;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

'use client';

import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useToastStore, type Toast as ToastType } from '@/store/toast-store';
import AlertV4 from './Alert';

interface ToastItemProps {
  toast: ToastType;
  onRemove: (id: string) => void;
}

function ToastItem({ toast, onRemove }: ToastItemProps) {
  const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(false);
  const [isLeaving, setIsLeaving] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    // Trigger enter animation
    const showTimer = setTimeout(() => setIsVisible(true), 10);

    // Auto-dismiss after duration
    const duration = toast.duration ?? 4000;
    const dismissTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      setIsLeaving(true);
      setTimeout(() => onRemove(toast.id), 300);
    }, duration);

    return () => {
      clearTimeout(showTimer);
      clearTimeout(dismissTimer);
    };
  }, [toast.id, toast.duration, onRemove]);

  const handleClose = () => {
    setIsLeaving(true);
    setTimeout(() => onRemove(toast.id), 300);
  };

  return (
    <div
      className={`
        transform transition-all duration-300 ease-out
        ${
          isVisible && !isLeaving
            ? 'translate-x-0 opacity-100'
            : '-translate-x-full opacity-0'
        }
      `}
    >
      <AlertV4
        type={toast.type}
        title={toast.title}
        onClose={handleClose}
        variant="soft"
        compact
        className="shadow-lg min-w-[280px] max-w-[380px]"
      >
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
          <span>{toast.message}</span>
          {toast.action && (
            <button
              onClick={() => {
                toast.action?.onClick();
                handleClose();
              }}
              className="self-start text-sm font-medium underline underline-offset-2 hover:no-underline transition-all"
            >
              {toast.action.label}
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </AlertV4>
    </div>
  );
}

export default function ToastContainer() {
  const toasts = useToastStore((state) => state.toasts);
  const removeToast = useToastStore((state) => state.removeToast);

  if (toasts.length === 0) return null;

  return (
    <div
      className="fixed z-[9999] flex flex-col gap-3 pointer-events-none right-4 top-4"
      aria-live="polite"
      aria-label="اعلان‌ها"
    >
      {toasts.map((toast) => (
        <div key={toast.id} className="pointer-events-auto">
          <ToastItem toast={toast} onRemove={removeToast} />
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

+import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest';
+import {
+  normalizeDigits,
+  containsRightToLeftCharacters,
+  isValidName,
+  normalizePhoneNumber,
+  isValidPhoneNumber,
+  getPhoneLookupCandidates,
+} from '@/lib/utils/text';
+
+describe('text utils', () => {
+  it('keeps ASCII digits unchanged', () => {
+    expect(normalizeDigits('1234567890')).toBe('1234567890');
+    expect(normalizeDigits('0123456789')).toBe('0123456789');
+  });
+
+  it('detects right-to-left characters', () => {
+    expect(
+      containsRightToLeftCharacters(
+        String.fromCharCode(0x0633, 0x0644, 0x0627, 0x0645)
+      )
+    ).toBe(true);
+    expect(containsRightToLeftCharacters('hello')).toBe(false);
+  });
+
+  it('validates international names', () => {
+    expect(isValidName('Alex Taylor')).toBe(true);
+    expect(isValidName("Ali O'Reilly")).toBe(true);
+    expect(isValidName('Maria Garcia')).toBe(true);
+    expect(isValidName('')).toBe(false);
+  });
+
+  it('normalizes phone numbers and validates international formats', () => {
+    const previousCountry = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY;
+    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY = 'US';
+
+    try {
+      expect(normalizePhoneNumber('+1 (212) 555-1234')).toBe('+12125551234');
+      expect(normalizePhoneNumber('2125551234')).toBe('+12125551234');
+      expect(isValidPhoneNumber('+12125551234')).toBe(true);
+      expect(isValidPhoneNumber('2125551234')).toBe(true);
+      expect(isValidPhoneNumber('12345')).toBe(false);
+    } finally {
+      if (previousCountry === undefined) {
+        delete process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY;
+      } else {
+        process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY = previousCountry;
+      }
+    }
+  });
+
+  it('keeps the existing national phone default until callers opt into another country', () => {
+    const previousCountry = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY;
+    delete process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY;
+
+    try {
+      expect(normalizePhoneNumber('09123456789')).toBe('+989123456789');
+      expect(isValidPhoneNumber('09123456789')).toBe(true);
+    } finally {
+      if (previousCountry !== undefined) {
+        process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY = previousCountry;
+      }
+    }
+  });
+
+  it('keeps legacy phone storage candidates for lookup compatibility', () => {
+    const previousCountry = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY;
+    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY = 'IR';
+
+    try {
+      expect(getPhoneLookupCandidates('۰۹۱۲۳۴۵۶۷۸۹')).toEqual([
+        '+989123456789',
+        '09123456789',
+      ]);
+      expect(getPhoneLookupCandidates('+989123456789')).toEqual([
+        '+989123456789',
+        '09123456789',
+        '989123456789',
+      ]);
+    } finally {
+      if (previousCountry === undefined) {
+        delete process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY;
+      } else {
+        process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_DEFAULT_PHONE_COUNTRY = previousCountry;
+      }
+    }
+  });
+});

     1	import { createClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';
     2	import { getPhoneLookupCandidates } from '@/lib/utils/text';
     3	
     4	/**
     5	 * User information type (without password)
     6	 */
     7	export type UserInfo = {
     8	  id: string;
     9	  uid: string;
    10	  email: string | null;
    11	  phone: string | null;
    12	  name: string;
    13	  role: 'USER' | 'ADMIN';
    14	  isVerified: boolean;
    15	  shippingAddress: string | null;
    16	  postalCode: string | null;
    17	  createdAt: Date;
    18	  updatedAt: Date;
    19	};
    20	
    21	/**
    22	 * Generic user query function
    23	 * Reduces duplication in getUserById, getUserByEmail, getUserByPhone
    24	 */
    25	export async function queryUser(where: {
    26	  id?: string;
    27	  email?: string;
    28	  phone?: string;
    29	}): Promise<UserInfo | null> {
    30	  const supabase = createClient();
    31	
    32	  let query = supabase
    33	    .from('users')
    34	    .select(
    35	      'id, uid, email, phone, name, role, isVerified, shippingAddress, postalCode, createdAt, updatedAt'
    36	    )
    37	    .limit(1);
    38	
    39	  if (where.id) {
    40	    query = query.eq('id', where.id);
    41	  } else if (where.email) {
    42	    query = query.eq('email', where.email);
    43	  } else if (where.phone) {
    44	    query = query.eq('phone', where.phone);
    45	  } else {
    46	    return null;
    47	  }
    48	
    49	  const { data, error } = await query.single();
    50	
    51	  if (error || !data) {
    52	    return null;
    53	  }
    54	
    55	  // Convert string dates to Date objects for type compatibility
    56	  return {
    57	    ...data,
    58	    createdAt: new Date(data.createdAt),
    59	    updatedAt: new Date(data.updatedAt),
    60	  };
    61	}
    62	
    63	/**
    64	 * Check if a user exists with the given identifier
    65	 * Used for uniqueness validation
    66	 */
    67	export async function checkUserExists(
    68	  identifier: { email?: string; phone?: string },
    69	  excludeUserId?: string
    70	): Promise<boolean> {
    71	  const supabase = createClient();
    72	
    73	  // Build OR conditions
    74	  const conditions = [];
    75	
    76	  if (identifier.email) {
    77	    conditions.push(`email.eq.${identifier.email}`);
    78	  }
    79	
    80	  if (identifier.phone) {
    81	    for (const phone of getPhoneLookupCandidates(identifier.phone)) {
    82	      conditions.push(`phone.eq.${phone}`);
    83	    }
    84	  }
    85	
    86	  if (conditions.length === 0) {
    87	    return false;
    88	  }
    89	
    90	  let query = supabase
    91	    .from('users')
    92	    .select('id', { count: 'exact', head: true })
    93	    .or(conditions.join(','));
    94	
    95	  if (excludeUserId) {
    96	    query = query.neq('id', excludeUserId);
    97	  }
    98	
    99	  const { count, error } = await query;
   100	
   101	  if (error) {
   102	    return false;
   103	  }
   104	
   105	  return (count ?? 0) > 0;
   106	}

    28	// POST /api/transactions/create - Create transaction and initiate payment
    29	async function postHandler(req: NextRequest) {
    30	  const startTime = Date.now();
    31	  // Extract client info for storing in transaction
    32	  const { ipAddress, userAgent } = getClientInfo(req);
    33	
    34	  try {
    35	    const session = await getServerSession(authOptions);
    36	    const body = await req.json();
    37	    const { items, shippingInfo, paymentMethod, promoCode } = body;
    38	
    39	    log.info('Transaction creation started', {
    40	      userId: session?.user?.id || 'guest',
    41	      itemCount: items?.length || 0,
    42	      paymentMethod: paymentMethod || 'STRIPE',
    43	      ip:
    44	        req.headers.get('x-forwarded-for') ||
    45	        req.headers.get('x-real-ip') ||
    46	        'unknown',
    47	    });
    48	
    49	    // Validate items
    50	    if (!items || !Array.isArray(items) || items.length === 0) {
    51	      return NextResponse.json(
    52	        { error: 'Your cart is empty.' },
    53	        { status: 400 }
    54	      );
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    for (const item of items) {
    58	      if (!item || typeof item.productId !== 'string' || !item.productId) {
    59	        return NextResponse.json(
    60	          { error: 'Cart items are invalid.' },
    61	          { status: 400 }
    62	        );
    63	      }
    64	
    65	      if (
    66	        item.variantId !== undefined &&
    67	        item.variantId !== null &&
    68	        typeof item.variantId !== 'string'
    69	      ) {
    70	        return NextResponse.json(
    71	          { error: 'Variant id is invalid.' },
    72	          { status: 400 }
    73	        );
    74	      }
    75	
    76	      const quantity = Number(item.quantity);
    77	      if (!Number.isInteger(quantity) || quantity <= 0) {
    78	        return NextResponse.json(
    79	          { error: 'Quantity must be a positive whole number.' },
    80	          { status: 400 }
    81	        );
    82	      }
    83	
    84	      item.quantity = quantity;
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    // Validate shipping info
    88	    if (!shippingInfo) {
    89	      return NextResponse.json(
    90	        { error: 'Shipping information is required.' },
    91	        { status: 400 }
    92	      );
    93	    }
    94	
    95	    // For logged-in users, merge profile data with form data
    96	    // Use profile data for non-null fields, allow form data to fill in null fields
    97	    let finalFullName: string;
    98	    let finalPhone: string;
    99	    let finalEmail: string | undefined;
   100	    let shouldUpdateProfile = false;
   101	
   102	    if (session?.user) {
   103	      // Use session data (already fresh from NextAuth)
   104	      const { fullName, phone, email } = shippingInfo;
   105	
   106	      // For logged-in users: Use session data if available, otherwise allow form data
   107	      // Priority: Session data > Form data > Error for required fields
   108	      finalFullName = session.user.name || fullName || '';
   109	      finalPhone = session.user.phone || phone || '';
   110	      finalEmail = session.user.email || email || undefined;
   111	
   112	      // Validate required fields
   113	      if (!finalFullName) {
   114	        return NextResponse.json(
   115	          { error: 'Please enter your full name.' },
   116	          { status: 400 }
   117	        );
   118	      }
   119	
   120	      if (!finalPhone) {
   121	        return NextResponse.json(
   122	          { error: 'Please enter your phone number.' },
   123	          { status: 400 }
   124	        );
   125	      }
   126	
   127	      // Check if we need to update profile with new values from form
   128	      if (!session.user.name && fullName) {
   129	        shouldUpdateProfile = true;
   130	      }
   131	      if (!session.user.phone && phone) {
   132	        shouldUpdateProfile = true;
   133	      }
   134	      if (!session.user.email && email) {
   135	        shouldUpdateProfile = true;
   136	      }
   137	
   138	      log.info('Using merged user data for transaction', {
   139	        userId: session.user.id,
   140	        finalPhone,
   141	        finalEmail,
   142	        fromProfile: {
   143	          name: !!session.user.name,
   144	          phone: !!session.user.phone,
   145	          email: !!session.user.email,
   146	        },
   147	        fromForm: {
   148	          name: !session.user.name && !!fullName,
   149	          phone: !session.user.phone && !!phone,
   150	          email: !session.user.email && !!email,
   151	        },
   152	        willUpdateProfile: shouldUpdateProfile,
   153	      });
   154	    } else {
   155	      // For guest users, use form data
   156	      const { fullName, phone, email } = shippingInfo;
   157	
   158	      if (!fullName || !phone) {
   159	        return NextResponse.json(
   160	          { error: 'Please complete all required fields.' },
   161	          { status: 400 }
   162	        );
   163	      }
   164	
   165	      finalFullName = fullName;
   166	      finalPhone = normalizePhoneNumber(phone);
   167	      finalEmail = email || undefined;
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    // Validate shipping address (both logged-in and guest users)
   171	    const { shippingAddress, postalCode, createAccount } = shippingInfo;
   172	
   173	    if (!shippingAddress) {
   174	      return NextResponse.json(
   175	        { error: 'Please enter a shipping address.' },
   176	        { status: 400 }
   177	      );
   178	    }
   179	
   180	    // Validate phone format
   181	    finalPhone = normalizePhoneNumber(finalPhone);
   182	    if (!isValidPhoneNumber(finalPhone)) {
   183	      return NextResponse.json(
   184	        { error: 'Invalid phone number format.' },
   185	        { status: 400 }
   186	      );
   187	    }
   188	
   189	    // Verify stock availability
   190	    const stockCheck = await verifyStockAvailability(items);
   191	    if (!stockCheck.available) {
   192	      log.warn('Stock verification failed', {
   193	        userId: session?.user?.id || 'guest',
   194	        errors: stockCheck.errors,
   195	        unavailableProductIds: stockCheck.unavailableProductIds,
   196	        items: items.map((i) => ({
   197	          productId: i.productId,
   198	          variantId: i.variantId,
   199	          quantity: i.quantity,
   200	        })),
   201	      });
   202	      return NextResponse.json(
   203	        {
   204	          error: 'Insufficient stock.',
   205	          details: stockCheck.errors,
   206	          unavailableProductIds: stockCheck.unavailableProductIds,
   207	        },
   208	        { status: 400 }
   209	      );
   210	    }
   211	
   212	    // Calculate total and prepare transaction items
   213	    let totalAmount = 0;
   214	    const transactionItems: Array<{
   215	      productId: string;
   216	      variantId?: string;
   217	      quantity: number;
   218	      price: number;
   219	    }> = [];
   220	
   221	    log.info('Starting price calculation for transaction items', {
   222	      userId: session?.user?.id || 'guest',
   223	      itemCount: items.length,
   224	      items: items.map((i) => ({
   225	        productId: i.productId,
   226	        variantId: i.variantId,
   227	        quantity: i.quantity,
   228	      })),
   229	    });

     2	import { createUser, detectIdentifierType } from '@/services/user-service';

    10	async function postHandler(req: NextRequest) {
    11	  // Extract client info for activity logging
    12	  const { ipAddress, userAgent } = getClientInfo(req);
    13	
    14	  try {
    15	    const body = await req.json();
    16	    const { identifier, email, phone, password, name } = body;
    17	    const providedIdentifier = identifier || email || phone;
    18	
    19	    // Validate required fields (name is optional)
    20	    if (!providedIdentifier || !password) {
    21	      return NextResponse.json(

    23	        { status: 400 }

    33	        { status: 400 }

    35	    }

    38	    // If name is not provided, use empty string as default
    39	    const user = await createUser({
    40	      email: identifierType === 'email' ? normalizedIdentifier : undefined,
    41	      phone: identifierType === 'phone' ? normalizedIdentifier : undefined,
    42	      password,
    43	      name: name || '',
    44	    });
    45	
    46	    // Log successful registration (fire-and-forget)
    47	    logUserActivity({
    48	      userId: user.id,
    49	      activityType: 'REGISTER',
    50	      ipAddress,
    51	      userAgent,
    52	      success: true,
    53	      metadata: {
    54	        identifier_type: identifierType,
    55	      },
    56	    }).catch((err) => {
    57	      log.warn('Failed to log registration', {
    58	        userId: user.id,
    59	        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
    60	      });
    61	    });
    62	
    63	    return NextResponse.json(
    64	      {
    65	        success: true,
    66	        message: 'ثبت‌نام با موفقیت انجام شد',
    67	        user: {
    68	          id: user.id,
    69	          email: user.email,
    70	          name: user.name,
    71	          role: user.role,
    72	        },
    73	      },
    74	      { status: 201 }
    75	    );
    76	  } catch (error) {
    77	    console.error('Registration error:', error);
    78	
    79	    // Log failed registration (fire-and-forget)
    80	    logUserActivity({
    81	      activityType: 'REGISTER',
    82	      ipAddress,
    83	      userAgent,
    84	      success: false,
    85	      errorMessage:
    86	        error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Registration failed',
    87	    }).catch((err) => {
    88	      log.warn('Failed to log registration failure', {
    89	        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
    90	      });

     8	export function validateEmail(email: string): boolean {
     9	  const emailRegex = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/;
    10	  return emailRegex.test(email);
    11	}
    12	
    13	export function validatePhone(phone: string): boolean {
    14	  return isValidPhoneNumber(phone);
    15	}
    16	
    17	/**
    18	 * Detect if input is email or phone
    19	 */
    20	export function detectIdentifierType(
    21	  identifier: string
    22	): 'email' | 'phone' | 'invalid' {
    23	  if (validateEmail(identifier)) return 'email';
    24	  if (validatePhone(identifier)) return 'phone';
    25	  return 'invalid';
    26	}
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * Validate and check uniqueness for email
    30	 * Throws error if invalid or already exists
    31	 */
    32	export async function validateEmailUniqueness(
    33	  email: string | undefined,
    34	  excludeUserId?: string
    35	): Promise<void> {
    36	  if (email === undefined) return;
    37	
    38	  // Validate format
    39	  if (email && !validateEmail(email)) {
    40	    log.warn('Invalid email format', { email });
    41	    throw new Error('فرمت ایمیل نامعتبر است');
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  // Check uniqueness
    45	  if (email) {
    46	    const exists = await checkUserExists({ email }, excludeUserId);
    47	    if (exists) {
    48	      log.warn('Email already in use', { email });
    49	      throw new Error('این ایمیل قبلاً استفاده شده است');
    50	    }
    51	  }
    52	}
    53	
    54	/**
    55	 * Validate and check uniqueness for phone
    56	 * Throws error if invalid or already exists
    57	 */
    58	export async function validatePhoneUniqueness(
    59	  phone: string | undefined,
    60	  excludeUserId?: string
    61	): Promise<void> {
    62	  if (phone === undefined) return;
    63	
    64	  const normalizedPhone = phone ? normalizePhoneNumber(phone) : undefined;
    65	
    66	  if (phone && !validatePhone(phone)) {
    67	    log.warn('Invalid phone format', { phone });
    68	    throw new Error('فرمت شماره تلفن نامعتبر است');
    69	  }
    70	
    71	  if (normalizedPhone) {
    72	    const exists = await checkUserExists(

    74	      excludeUserId
    75	    );

    77	      log.warn('Phone already in use', { phone: normalizedPhone });

    79	    }
    80	  }

# task006: Locale Direction And Currency Foundation

Status: Finalized with review blocker

## Goal

Replace Persian-first locale, font, date, currency, and direction assumptions with configurable English-default settings that still support both LTR and RTL layouts.

## Start Here

- Read `tasks/open-source-boilerplate-conversion/handoff.md`.
- Read `/home/dexter/.shared-agent-skills/codex-review-mode/SKILL.md`.

## Files To Inspect First

- `src/app/layout.tsx`
- `src/app/globals.css`
- `tailwind.config.ts`
- `config/tailwind.config.ts`
- `src/config/site.ts`
- `src/lib/utils/format.ts`
- `src/store/cart-store.ts`
- `src/lib/utils/persian.ts`
- files importing `date-fns-jalali`
- `package.json`
- `public/fonts/BYekan.ttf`

## Requirements

- Create or update a central locale/site configuration for `language`, `direction`, `locale`, `currency`, and display name.
- Default to English, LTR, and USD, while preserving an easy path to set RTL direction.
- Replace hard-coded `lang="fa"` and `dir="rtl"` with config-driven values.
- Replace `fa-IR`, `fa_IR`, Toman strings, and Jalali date formatting with config-driven or standard `Intl` formatting.
- Remove `date-fns-jalali` and `BYekan.ttf` if no longer used.
- Rename `src/lib/utils/persian.ts` to a neutral utility module or split digit/phone/name helpers into generic utilities.
- Keep CSS compatible with both LTR and RTL. Prefer logical spacing/alignment where feasible.

## Acceptance Criteria

- App default renders as English/LTR without Persian font dependency.
- Currency formatting works from one shared utility.
- Date formatting no longer depends on Jalali defaults.
- `rg -n "fa-IR|fa_IR|date-fns-jalali|BYekan|تومان|ریال|lang=\"fa\"|dir=\"rtl\"" src package.json tailwind.config.ts config/tailwind.config.ts public` returns no default Persian-first assumptions. Intentional RTL support may remain if config-driven and documented.

     8	// Minimal product interface for schema generation
     9	interface SchemaProduct {
    10	  id: string;
    11	  name: string;
    12	  description: string;
    13	  slug?: string; // Optional, will use id if not present
    14	  price: number;
    15	  stock: number;
    16	  discount?: number | null;
    17	  discountPercent?: number | null;
    18	  sku?: string | null;
    19	  images?: string[] | null;
    20	  category?: { name: string; slug: string } | null;
    21	  media?: Array<{ url: string; type?: string }>;
    22	  variants?: Array<{ media?: Array<{ url: string; type?: string }> }>;
    23	}
    24	
    25	// Minimal variant interface for schema generation
    26	interface SchemaVariant {
    27	  name: string;
    28	  stock: number;
    29	  priceAdjust: number;
    30	  media?: Array<{ url: string; type?: string }>;
    31	}
    32	
    33	// Get base URL from environment or default
    34	const getBaseUrl = (): string => {
    35	  if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
    36	    return window.location.origin;
    37	  }
    38	  return process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL || 'https://kitia.ir';
    39	};
    40	
    41	/**
    42	 * Generate Product JSON-LD structured data
    43	 * Creates rich snippet for product pages with offers, images, and ratings
    44	 */
    45	export function generateProductSchema(
    46	  product: SchemaProduct,
    47	  selectedVariant?: SchemaVariant
    48	): object {
    49	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
    50	
    51	  // Get images from product media or variant media
    52	  const images: string[] = [];
    53	
    54	  if (selectedVariant?.media && selectedVariant.media.length > 0) {
    55	    // Use selected variant's media
    56	    const variantImages = selectedVariant.media
    57	      .filter((m) => m.type === 'IMAGE' || !m.type)
    58	      .map((m) => m.url);
    59	    images.push(...variantImages);
    60	  } else if (product.media && product.media.length > 0) {
    61	    // Use product-level media
    62	    const productImages = product.media
    63	      .filter((m) => m.type === 'IMAGE' || !m.type)
    64	      .map((m) => m.url);
    65	    images.push(...productImages);
    66	  } else if (product.images && product.images.length > 0) {
    67	    // Use legacy images field
    68	    images.push(...product.images);
    69	  } else if (product.variants && product.variants.length > 0) {
    70	    // Fallback: collect images from all variants if product has no direct media
    71	    for (const variant of product.variants) {
    72	      if (variant.media && variant.media.length > 0) {
    73	        const variantImages = variant.media
    74	          .filter((m) => m.type === 'IMAGE' || !m.type)
    75	          .map((m) => m.url);
    76	        images.push(...variantImages);
    77	      }
    78	    }
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  // Calculate final price (with variant adjustment if applicable)
    82	  let finalPrice = product.price;
    83	  if (selectedVariant) {
    84	    finalPrice += selectedVariant.priceAdjust;
    85	  }
    86	
    87	  // Apply discount if exists
    88	  if (product.discount && product.discount > 0) {
    89	    finalPrice = finalPrice * (1 - product.discount / 100);
    90	  }
    91	
    92	  // Determine stock availability
    93	  let stock = product.stock;
    94	  if (selectedVariant) {
    95	    stock = selectedVariant.stock;
    96	  }
    97	
    98	  const availability =
    99	    stock > 0 ? 'https://schema.org/InStock' : 'https://schema.org/OutOfStock';
   100	
   101	  // Schema.org requires at least one image - use logo as absolute last resort
   102	  const schemaImages = images.length > 0 ? images : [`${baseUrl}/logo.png`];
   103	
   104	  const schema = {
   105	    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
   106	    '@type': 'Product',
   107	    name: selectedVariant
   108	      ? `${product.name} - ${selectedVariant.name}`
   109	      : product.name,
   110	    description: product.description || `${product.name} - ${siteConfig.name}`,
   111	    image: schemaImages,
   112	    ...(product.sku && { sku: product.sku }),
   113	    brand: {
   114	      '@type': 'Brand',
   115	      name: siteConfig.name,
   116	    },
   117	    offers: {
   118	      '@type': 'Offer',
   119	      price: finalPrice.toString(),
   120	      priceCurrency: siteLocale.currency,
   121	      availability,
   122	      url: `${baseUrl}/products/${product.slug || product.id}`,
   123	      ...(product.discount &&
   124	        product.discount > 0 && {
   125	          priceValidUntil: new Date(
   126	            Date.now() + 30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000
   127	          ).toISOString(), // 30 days
   128	        }),
   129	    },
   130	  };
   131	
   132	  return schema;
   133	}

   135	/**
   136	 * Generate Organization JSON-LD structured data
   137	 * Should be included in the root layout for site-wide branding
   138	 */
   139	export function generateOrganizationSchema(): object {
   140	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
   141	
   142	  return {
   143	    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
   144	    '@type': 'Organization',
   145	    name: siteConfig.name,
   146	    url: baseUrl,
   147	    logo: `${baseUrl}/logo.png`,
   148	    description: siteConfig.description,
   149	    contactPoint: {
   150	      '@type': 'ContactPoint',
   151	      contactType: 'customer support',
   152	      availableLanguage: siteLocale.language,
   153	    },
   154	  };
   155	}
   156	
   157	/**
   158	 * Generate BreadcrumbList JSON-LD structured data
   159	 * Shows navigation hierarchy (Home > Category > Subcategory > Product)
   160	 */
   161	export function generateBreadcrumbSchema(items: BreadcrumbItem[]): object {
   162	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
   163	
   164	  const listItems = items.map((item, index) => ({
   165	    '@type': 'ListItem',
   166	    position: index + 1,
   167	    name: item.name,
   168	    item: item.url.startsWith('http') ? item.url : `${baseUrl}${item.url}`,
   169	  }));
   170	
   171	  return {
   172	    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
   173	    '@type': 'BreadcrumbList',
   174	    itemListElement: listItems,
   175	  };
   176	}
   177	
   178	/**
   179	 * Generate breadcrumb items for a product page
   180	 * Includes category hierarchy if available
   181	 */
   182	export function generateProductBreadcrumbs(
   183	  product: SchemaProduct,
   184	  categoryHierarchy?: Array<{ name: string; slug: string }>
   185	): BreadcrumbItem[] {
   186	  const items: BreadcrumbItem[] = [
   187	    {
   188	      name: 'Home',
   189	      url: '/',
   190	    },
   191	  ];
   192	
   193	  // Add category hierarchy if provided
   194	  if (categoryHierarchy && categoryHierarchy.length > 0) {
   195	    categoryHierarchy.forEach((category) => {
   196	      items.push({
   197	        name: category.name,
   198	        url: `/products?category=${category.slug}`,
   199	      });
   200	    });
   201	  } else if (product.category) {
   202	    // Fallback to just the direct category
   203	    items.push({
   204	      name: product.category.name,
   205	      url: `/products?category=${product.category.slug}`,
   206	    });
   207	  }
   208	
   209	  // Add the product itself
   210	  items.push({
   211	    name: product.name,
   212	    url: `/products/${product.slug || product.id}`,
   213	  });
   214	
   215	  return items;
   216	}
   217	
   218	/**
   219	 * Generate WebSite JSON-LD structured data
   220	 * Includes site search capability
   221	 */
   222	export function generateWebSiteSchema(): object {
   223	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
   224	
   225	  return {
   226	    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
   227	    '@type': 'WebSite',
   228	    name: siteConfig.name,
   229	    url: baseUrl,
   230	    potentialAction: {
   231	      '@type': 'SearchAction',
   232	      target: {
   233	        '@type': 'EntryPoint',
   234	        urlTemplate: `${baseUrl}/products?search={search_term_string}`,
   235	      },
   236	      'query-input': 'required name=search_term_string',
   237	    },
   238	  };
   239	}

   243	 * Returns a script tag with type="application/ld+json"

   245	export function renderJsonLd(data: object): string {

   158	 * Generate BreadcrumbList JSON-LD structured data
   159	 * Shows navigation hierarchy (Home > Category > Subcategory > Product)
   160	 */
   161	export function generateBreadcrumbSchema(items: BreadcrumbItem[]): object {
   162	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
   163	
   164	  const listItems = items.map((item, index) => ({
   165	    '@type': 'ListItem',
   166	    position: index + 1,
   167	    name: item.name,
   168	    item: item.url.startsWith('http') ? item.url : `${baseUrl}${item.url}`,
   169	  }));
   170	
   171	  return {
   172	    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
   173	    '@type': 'BreadcrumbList',
   174	    itemListElement: listItems,
   175	  };
   176	}
   177	
   178	/**
   179	 * Generate breadcrumb items for a product page
   180	 * Includes category hierarchy if available
   181	 */
   182	export function generateProductBreadcrumbs(
   183	  product: SchemaProduct,
   184	  categoryHierarchy?: Array<{ name: string; slug: string }>
   185	): BreadcrumbItem[] {
   186	  const items: BreadcrumbItem[] = [
   187	    {
   188	      name: 'Home',
   189	      url: '/',
   190	    },
   191	  ];
   192	
   193	  // Add category hierarchy if provided
   194	  if (categoryHierarchy && categoryHierarchy.length > 0) {
   195	    categoryHierarchy.forEach((category) => {
   196	      items.push({
   197	        name: category.name,
   198	        url: `/products?category=${category.slug}`,
   199	      });
   200	    });
   201	  } else if (product.category) {
   202	    // Fallback to just the direct category
   203	    items.push({
   204	      name: product.category.name,
   205	      url: `/products?category=${product.category.slug}`,
   206	    });
   207	  }
   208	
   209	  // Add the product itself
   210	  items.push({
   211	    name: product.name,
   212	    url: `/products/${product.slug || product.id}`,
   213	  });
   214	
   215	  return items;
   216	}
   217	
   218	/**
   219	 * Generate WebSite JSON-LD structured data
   220	 * Includes site search capability
   221	 */
   222	export function generateWebSiteSchema(): object {
   223	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
   224	
   225	  return {
   226	    '@context': 'https://schema.org',
   227	    '@type': 'WebSite',
   228	    name: siteConfig.name,
   229	    url: baseUrl,
   230	    potentialAction: {
   231	      '@type': 'SearchAction',
   232	      target: {
   233	        '@type': 'EntryPoint',
   234	        urlTemplate: `${baseUrl}/products?search={search_term_string}`,
   235	      },
   236	      'query-input': 'required name=search_term_string',
   237	    },
   238	  };
   239	}
   240	
   241	/**
   242	 * Helper function to inject JSON-LD script into the page
   243	 * Returns a script tag with type="application/ld+json"
   244	 */
   245	export function renderJsonLd(data: object): string {
   246	  return JSON.stringify(data);
   247	}

  'bif',

let stripeClient: Stripe | null = null;

interface StripeCheckoutSessionRequest {

function getStripeSecretKey(): string {
  const secretKey = process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY;

  if (!secretKey) {
    throw new Error('STRIPE_SECRET_KEY is not configured');
  }

  return secretKey;
}

function getStripeWebhookSecret(): string {
  const webhookSecret = process.env.STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET;

  if (!webhookSecret) {
    throw new Error('STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET is not configured');
  }

  return webhookSecret;
}

function getNormalizedBaseUrl(): string {
  const baseUrl = getAppBaseUrl();
  return baseUrl.endsWith('/') ? baseUrl.slice(0, -1) : baseUrl;
}

export function getStripeCurrency(): string {
  return (process.env.STRIPE_CURRENCY || 'usd').toLowerCase();
}

export function toStripeMinorUnits(amount: number, currency: string): number {
  if (!Number.isFinite(amount) || amount <= 0) {
    throw new Error('Stripe amount must be a positive number');
  }

  const normalizedCurrency = currency.toLowerCase();
  const usesZeroDecimal = ZERO_DECIMAL_CURRENCIES.has(normalizedCurrency);

  return usesZeroDecimal ? Math.round(amount) : Math.round(amount * 100);
}

export function getStripeClient(): Stripe {
  if (!stripeClient) {
    stripeClient = new Stripe(getStripeSecretKey(), {
      typescript: true,
    });
  }

  return stripeClient;
}

    33	/**
    34	 * Calculate discounted price
    35	 */
    36	export function calculateDiscountedPrice(
    37	  basePrice: number,
    38	  discountPercent: number | null | undefined
    39	): number {
    40	  if (!discountPercent || discountPercent <= 0) {
    41	    return basePrice;
    42	  }
    43	  return basePrice * (1 - discountPercent / 100);
    44	}

Identified test/UI mismatch and phone normalization compatibility risks; preparing final JSON.
  ✓ Inspect commit diff and affected files
  ✓ Analyze runtime impact and affected call sites
  → Produce prioritized JSON review findings
codex
The patch introduces a compatibility break for existing phone-based accounts and updates smoke tests to expect English UI that the app does not yet render. These are functional regressions that should be addressed before the change is considered correct.

Full review comments:

- [P1] Preserve lookups for previously stored phone numbers — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/services/auth-service.ts:43-46
  For deployments with users created before this commit, phone rows were stored as the submitted local value (for example `09123456789`). This new lookup normalizes an entered phone to the configured international value (for example `+989123456789` when IR is configured, or rejects `09...` with the new US default), but there is no data migration or fallback query for the old value, so existing phone-only users cannot log in and guest transaction linking misses their prior rows.

- [P2] Align smoke assertions with untranslated UI — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/tests/e2e/smoke.spec.ts:10-10
  With this commit, `/` still uses hard-coded Kitia metadata in `src/app/page.tsx` and the header/cart components still expose Persian accessible names, so these new English smoke assertions fail in any E2E run of the current app; the later `Supabase Vercel Stack`, `Cart`, and `Your cart is empty` selectors have the same problem. Either wire the UI to `siteConfig`/translations in this change or keep the assertions matching the current UI.
The patch introduces a compatibility break for existing phone-based accounts and updates smoke tests to expect English UI that the app does not yet render. These are functional regressions that should be addressed before the change is considered correct.

Full review comments:

- [P1] Preserve lookups for previously stored phone numbers — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/services/auth-service.ts:43-46
  For deployments with users created before this commit, phone rows were stored as the submitted local value (for example `09123456789`). This new lookup normalizes an entered phone to the configured international value (for example `+989123456789` when IR is configured, or rejects `09...` with the new US default), but there is no data migration or fallback query for the old value, so existing phone-only users cannot log in and guest transaction linking misses their prior rows.

- [P2] Align smoke assertions with untranslated UI — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/tests/e2e/smoke.spec.ts:10-10
  With this commit, `/` still uses hard-coded Kitia metadata in `src/app/page.tsx` and the header/cart components still expose Persian accessible names, so these new English smoke assertions fail in any E2E run of the current app; the later `Supabase Vercel Stack`, `Cart`, and `Your cart is empty` selectors have the same problem. Either wire the UI to `siteConfig`/translations in this change or keep the assertions matching the current UI.

codex
The patch introduces English/USD defaults but leaves customer-facing currency output and route metadata hard-coded to Persian/Toman in important flows. Those inconsistencies mean the locale/currency foundation is not correct for the default configuration.

Full review comments:

- [P2] Migrate receipt and promo currency formatting — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/config/site.ts:15-15
  With the new default `NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_CURRENCY` fallbacking to USD, checkout/product/admin screens display USD via `formatPrice`, but order emails and promo-code minimum errors still format the same amounts with hard-coded `toLocaleString('fa-IR') + ' تومان'` in `src/lib/email/client.ts` and `src/services/promo-service.ts`. In a default install, customers can complete checkout in USD and then receive receipts/errors in Toman, so route those currency strings through the shared formatter before switching the site default.

- [P2] Use configured locale in remaining metadata — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/config/site.ts:14-14
  With `siteConfig.locale` now defaulting to `en-US` and product detail metadata using `siteLocale`, the rest of the route metadata still hard-codes `openGraph.locale: 'fa_IR'` in pages like home, products listing, cart, and static pages, while `src/lib/seo/config.ts` keeps the same default. In the default English install, crawlers/social cards see conflicting `html lang="en"` and `og:locale=fa_IR`, so migrate those metadata helpers/pages to `siteLocale.ogLocale` or keep the root locale unchanged until they are migrated.
The patch introduces English/USD defaults but leaves customer-facing currency output and route metadata hard-coded to Persian/Toman in important flows. Those inconsistencies mean the locale/currency foundation is not correct for the default configuration.
